sql 구문는 아래와 같으며, JPA이랑 Mybatis 공용으로 DB를 사용함(Mybatis랑 JPA같이사용하는것을 학원에서 요청한 사항, 추후에는 같이 사용하지 말 것)

// DB 정보 | oracle 11g,  버전 23.1.0.097, 빌드 097.1607
//Java(TM) 플랫폼	12.0.2
//Oracle IDE	23.1.0.097.1607
//버전 지정 지원	23.1.0.097.1607

--  파일이 생성됨 - 월요일-1월-29-2024   
--------------------------------------------------------
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Sequence EDITREQUESTID_SEQ
--------------------------------------------------------

   CREATE SEQUENCE  "CHATPTDB"."EDITREQUESTID_SEQ"  MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 10000000000000 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 82 NOCACHE  NOORDER  NOCYCLE ;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Sequence EIDTREQUEST_SEQ
--------------------------------------------------------

   CREATE SEQUENCE  "CHATPTDB"."EIDTREQUEST_SEQ"  MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999999999999999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 CACHE 20 NOORDER  NOCYCLE ;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Sequence FOOD_SEQ
--------------------------------------------------------

   CREATE SEQUENCE  "CHATPTDB"."FOOD_SEQ"  MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999999999999999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 401 CACHE 20 NOORDER  NOCYCLE ;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Sequence MYCALENDAR_SEQ
--------------------------------------------------------

   CREATE SEQUENCE  "CHATPTDB"."MYCALENDAR_SEQ"  MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999999999999999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 53 CACHE 20 NOORDER  NOCYCLE ;
--------------------------------------------------------

   CREATE SEQUENCE  "CHATPTDB"."NORMAL_MEM_SEQ"  MINVALUE 432 MAXVALUE 9999999999999999999999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 534 CACHE 20 NOORDER  NOCYCLE ;

--  DDL for Table CHATLOG
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE TABLE "CHATPTDB"."CHATLOG" 
   (	"SENDER" VARCHAR2(255 BYTE), 
	"LOGDATE" DATE, 
	"ROOMID" VARCHAR2(255 BYTE), 
	"MESSAGE" CLOB, 
	"TYPE" VARCHAR2(20 BYTE)
   ) SEGMENT CREATION IMMEDIATE 
  PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "SYSTEM" 
 LOB ("MESSAGE") STORE AS BASICFILE (
  TABLESPACE "SYSTEM" ENABLE STORAGE IN ROW CHUNK 8192 RETENTION 
  NOCACHE LOGGING 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)) ;

   COMMENT ON COLUMN "CHATPTDB"."CHATLOG"."SENDER" IS '메시지 보낸사람
';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "CHATPTDB"."CHATLOG"."LOGDATE" IS '보낸 시간';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "CHATPTDB"."CHATLOG"."ROOMID" IS '채팅방아이디';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "CHATPTDB"."CHATLOG"."MESSAGE" IS '메세지 내용';
   COMMENT ON COLUMN "CHATPTDB"."CHATLOG"."TYPE" IS '메시지 보내는방식
';
   COMMENT ON TABLE "CHATPTDB"."CHATLOG"  IS '메세지 로그';

 LOB ("TRAINERINTRO") STORE AS BASICFILE (

--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Procedure GET_CONSECUTIVE_DATES
--------------------------------------------------------
set define off;

  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "CHATPTDB"."GET_CONSECUTIVE_DATES" (
    p_id IN normal_mem.normal_id%TYPE,
    P_COUNT OUT NUMBER
) AS
  v_first_uploaddate DATE;
  v_current_date DATE;
  v_count NUMBER;

BEGIN
  -- 첫 업로드 날짜를 구합니다.
  SELECT TRUNC(MIN(u.uploaddate))
  INTO v_first_uploaddate
  FROM upphoto u
  INNER JOIN normal_mem n ON u.nnum = n.nnum
  WHERE n.normal_id = p_id;

  P_COUNT := 0;
  v_current_date := v_first_uploaddate;

  -- 현재 날짜부터 시작해서 첫 번째 빈 날짜가 나타날 때까지 반복
  WHILE v_current_date < TRUNC(SYSDATE) LOOP
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    INTO v_count
    FROM upphoto u
    INNER JOIN normal_mem n ON u.nnum = n.nnum
    WHERE n.normal_id = p_id AND TRUNC(u.uploaddate) = TRUNC(v_current_date);

    -- 데이터가 있는 날짜면 카운트를 증가시킵니다.
    IF v_count > 0 THEN
      P_COUNT := P_COUNT + 1;
    -- 데이터가 없으면 반복을 중단합니다.
    ELSE
      P_COUNT := 0;
    END IF;

    -- 다음 날짜로 이동합니다.
    v_current_date := v_current_date + 1;
  END LOOP;
  SELECT COUNT(*)
    INTO v_count
    FROM upphoto u
    INNER JOIN normal_mem n ON u.nnum = n.nnum
    WHERE n.normal_id = p_id AND TRUNC(u.uploaddate) = TRUNC(sysdate);
    IF v_count>0 then
        P_COUNT := P_COUNT + 1;
    ELSE
        P_COUNT :=0;
    END IF;
END;

/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Procedure GET_RECOMMAND_CAL
--------------------------------------------------------
set define off;

  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "CHATPTDB"."GET_RECOMMAND_CAL" (
    p_id IN members.id%TYPE,
    p_recommand_cal OUT NUMBER
) AS
v_age NUMBER;
v_gender members.gender%TYPE;
v_weight normal_mem.weight%TYPE;
v_height normal_mem.height%TYPE;
v_activity normal_mem.activity%TYPE;
v_purpose normal_mem.purpose%TYPE;
BEGIN
    SELECT FLOOR(MONTHS_BETWEEN(SYSDATE, m.BIRTH) / 12), m.gender, n.weight, n.height, n.activity, n.purpose
    INTO v_age, v_gender, v_weight, v_height, v_activity, v_purpose
    FROM members m
    INNER JOIN normal_mem n ON m.id = n.normal_id
    WHERE m.ID = p_id;

    IF v_gender = 'Male' THEN
        p_recommand_cal := 88.362 + (13.397 * v_weight) + (4.799 * v_height) - (5.677 * v_age);
    ELSE
        p_recommand_cal := 447.593 + (9.247 * v_weight) + (3.098 * v_height) - (4.330 * v_age);
    END IF;

    IF v_activity = 0 THEN
        p_recommand_cal := p_recommand_cal * 1.375;
    ELSIF v_activity = 1 THEN
        p_recommand_cal := p_recommand_cal * 1.55;
    ELSE 
        p_recommand_cal := p_recommand_cal * 1.725;
    END IF;

    IF v_purpose = 0 THEN
        p_recommand_cal := p_recommand_cal - 500;
    ELSIF v_purpose = 1 THEN
        p_recommand_cal := p_recommand_cal;
    ELSE 
        p_recommand_cal := p_recommand_cal + 500;
    END IF;
END;

/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Procedure GET_RECOMMAND_TANDANGI
--------------------------------------------------------
set define off;

  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "CHATPTDB"."GET_RECOMMAND_TANDANGI" (
    p_id IN members.id%TYPE,
    p_recommand_cal out number,
    p_recommand_tan OUT NUMBER,
    p_recommand_dan OUT NUMBER,
    p_recommand_gi OUT NUMBER
) AS
v_age NUMBER;
v_gender members.gender%TYPE;
v_weight normal_mem.weight%TYPE;
v_height normal_mem.height%TYPE;
v_activity normal_mem.activity%TYPE;
v_purpose normal_mem.purpose%TYPE;
BEGIN
    SELECT FLOOR(MONTHS_BETWEEN(SYSDATE, m.BIRTH) / 12), m.gender, n.weight, n.height, n.activity, n.purpose
    INTO v_age, v_gender, v_weight, v_height, v_activity, v_purpose
    FROM members m
    INNER JOIN normal_mem n ON m.id = n.normal_id
    WHERE m.ID = p_id;

    IF v_gender = 'Male' THEN
        p_recommand_cal := 88.362 + (13.397 * v_weight) + (4.799 * v_height) - (5.677 * v_age);
    ELSE
        p_recommand_cal := 447.593 + (9.247 * v_weight) + (3.098 * v_height) - (4.330 * v_age);
    END IF;

    IF v_activity = 0 THEN
        p_recommand_cal := p_recommand_cal * 1.375;
    ELSIF v_activity = 1 THEN
        p_recommand_cal := p_recommand_cal * 1.55;
    ELSE 
        p_recommand_cal := p_recommand_cal * 1.725;
    END IF;

    IF v_purpose = 0 THEN
        p_recommand_cal := p_recommand_cal - 500;
        p_recommand_tan := (p_recommand_cal * 0.40)/4;
        p_recommand_dan := (p_recommand_cal * 0.33)/4;
        p_recommand_gi := (p_recommand_cal * 0.27)/9;
    ELSIF v_purpose = 1 THEN
        p_recommand_cal := p_recommand_cal;
        p_recommand_tan := (p_recommand_cal * 0.45)/4;
        p_recommand_dan := (p_recommand_cal * 0.25)/4;
        p_recommand_gi := (p_recommand_cal * 0.30)/9;
    ELSE 
        p_recommand_cal := p_recommand_cal + 500;
        p_recommand_tan := (p_recommand_cal * 0.40)/4;
        p_recommand_dan := (p_recommand_cal * 0.30)/4;
        p_recommand_gi := (p_recommand_cal * 0.30)/9;
    END IF;
END;

	  REFERENCES "CHATPTDB"."FOOD" ("FOODNUM") ENABLE;
